agnivetAla is one of 8 kShetrapAla-s associated with the eastern reflex of the dakShiNAMnAya: hetuka, tripuraghna, agnijihva, agnivetAla, kAla, karAlaka, ekapAda, bhImanAtha. Further, we suspect that hetuka has an equivalence with heruka, who was prominent at the cemetery at kAmAkhyA and is worshiped in a great li~Nga.
